Title: The Comeback

So, picking up from where we left off. I arrive to Uruguay, but the boat that took me here was retarded, meaning that it was delayed, or tardy as some people may say. My mom was also delayed, which wasn't helping. She eventually arrived and picked me up. Then we went directly to the Uruguayan American School's anual alumni reunion to reunite with my old friends. Bruno called me and I confirmed to him that I was coming, I told him to blame fabrizzio for my lateness since his family owns the buquebus boat buisness.

Once I arrive, I saw Fede who was on his way out. He had a birthday, but we agreed to meet up someday, he is leaving this country once again on the 29nth. Upon entering the UAS confines and heading to the reunion area, I meet Lupi, Fabri, Luca Cassoni, Lucas, Bruno, Chiara, and last but certaintly not least, some people would actually say most, Daniiiiiiii. I however, DO NOT, meet Raz who had previously promised me that he was going to be here. This tells me that his promises are subject to changes which is not a good quality for promises to have.

We catch up and everything is super cool and really great. Bruno has an entire new look with a beard and a mustache he actually looks so epic. I also talked to Bruno about some really interesting developments in the recent war in the middle east. We are both on the same page regarding our opinions about it, we both think Hamas is a terrible terrorist organisation and the Israeli government is an equally terrible organisation full of war criminals, and both sides harbor so much hatred and animosity towards each other that it's borderline immpossible for any of them to reach any peacefull resolution. It's specially funny how both sides think that the opposite side has a very big grasp on social media and "rules the world", I knew about the classic "Jews run the world" type shi, but apparently the opposite also exists, like Hamas runs the world or the media or whatever.

We also talk about the new Chilean president, many of my chilean aquaintances on instagram are really not happy about the new president because he doesn't like gay people. It's just really sad that people in the right always harbor so much hatred for minorities because their policies aren't even that bad. but yeah he wants to end gay marriage and abortions.

Bruno also informs me that Sofe the future Film-maker was actually planning to go to this Alumni reunion, something that absolutely baffled me since she was living in France. Why would you want to leave, but apparently she appreciates her country of origin a lot, which is really respectable. Unfortunately she wasn't able to make a comeback because her flight got delayed in madrid. Federico Berman's flight also got delayed in madrid, so there is something going on in there.

Then I went to try to get a volleyball, on the way there crossing paths with Martina who didn't seem very happy to see me for some reason. I Mariela, mother of Luca taccone for a volleyball, and they gave us one, and we tried playing volleyball but failing miserable because Bruno couldn't really pass it that well.

We ate pizza and talked about a bunch of stuff. Chiara mentioned something about Martina doing something 16 times, and she also said they no longer hate each other, which is good. Basically they met at a birthday party because they were friends with Santino, they both speak english too so thats cool.

Mono and me

Lupi is also here, and he is really cool I like that he is here and I hope to see him more often. Chiara remarks how Lupi still has his chisled musculature, and she asks if Lupi still goes to the gym, he does indeed still go to the gym, he actually establishes he went today to the gym with Dani and probably someone else. I would like to join them but i'd be a little embarassed, i'll train by myself until I get strong enouph to not be embarassed.

Chiara and I eat a margarita pizza with spicy honey, everyone also eats some pizza. Chiara and Martina still enjoy of the pleasures of Nicotine, a habit that I was hoping was left in the past. But there is more to Lupi than what I previously mentioned, he also has a Cassino check that is apparently about to expire, so he has to go to redeem it. We all go to the gas station where Nico and I both get chocky milk, and then we head to the cassino. We all go to the bathroom, and we also meet jeff who was gambling in a suit. Jeff is our previous gym teacher back in UAS. He always made this very off-putting comments about girls... that were underaged. We then proceed to go to a bar because Mati and his roomate are there. Chiara, Martina, Nico, and Belu go with Chiara, while the rest go with fabri. We go there, but before getting out of the car they ask me to put Freestyle by lil baby.

Date: 21/12/2025

Climate: Sunny

Initial Spacetime: Unknown

Title: Sofe's comeback

Today we are meeting sofe for the first time in a long time. Upon waking up I created this little Document stored in a Portable Format that contains just about all of my thoughts about Raz, Sofe, and Fede and how they all hate each other and why. I love writing down my thoughs and analysing everything. And I feel like I have most definately reached a conclusion about the current war in the middle east. They all deserve to die, well actually no, if it were up to me no one would die. But if anyone dies it should be the people that are okay with killing others. The bad thing is the fact that it's not only the Hamas members and the Israeli goverment members that will suffer, all the innocent lives in-between. They are the real victims of the nonsensical war wagered by the evil forces of the Isaeli government and Hamas, and since they hate each other so much, there is no hope of this ending in any other way than one group, or the other, or perhaps both, disapearing, until only reasonable people exist. I guess it's the world's way of purging this nonsense, sacrificing thousands of innocent lives to get rid of the not-so-innocent lives. Well boy am I glad I have absolutely nothing to see, do, or care about in the middle of the east.

Anyways, after creating that awesome Document I asked Sofe where we were meeting up, the answer is in Punta gorda, immediately making me think of Fede and how much of a terrible idea it would be to invite him into this.

Lucas wants to go to the gym, but it's already 16:15 21/12/2025, So I don't know how he is planning to get to Punta Gorda at 18:00 21/12/2025, but I believe in him.

Before the main event of the day happened, I got in a call with Raz. This proved to be quite interesting. At first it was nothing out of the ordinary, he was just playing silksong after beating it for the first time. However then he said "You want to watch a lore video about why Islam's hate dogs". It was so random I failed to register it correctly three times in a row, also the mic cut a lot. I then confront Raz about his beliefs on the Islam population for the first time, by saying "I feel like you have some animosity towards this religion" he responded saying something along the lines of "Look, im just saying I don't like pedophiles and [something else that was bad but I don't remember]"

Then we proceeded to watch the video. The video doesn't actually attempt to give any explanation as to why Islams hate dogs, instead it's basically a huge compilation of quotes from the Qu'ran(Islam bible) aswell as some Hadiths(Muhammed quotes) that talk bad about dogs. Now to trust some random youtuber to succesfully interpret a religious text by just grabbing random quotes from such religious text and pointing out bad things... I know how it feels to be a victim of that because everyone does it with the religious text of my religion, AKA The Bible. And myriads of others also do it with The Torah and The Qu'ran. If we are going to just start picking bad verses we can mention how the Torah establishes you can rape women to force them to marry them or how the bible is A-Okay with slave trade. But if we want to get to some actual truth, then we might have to look at the context behind all of these quotes, and analyse the authors intent through the use of several lenses, most importantly the historical lense, seeing what were the values and beliefs of everyone at the time and stuff like that. Many people would say that is some very "woke" vocabulary I just used there, but I'd rather be woke than sleeping while analysing a text.

This video seemed to have one purpose only, to fuel a pre-existing hatred for a group of people. And I just really didn't like that, however I was way too occupied with other things to properly confront Raz about this behaviour. It's not even that I think that Islams are perfect, I despise the way they treat women, and the few Islam extremists do use these quotes as justifications for doing horrible things to dogs without any attempt to understand or correctly interpret their religion.

I won't say that I am an expert in the Qu'ran or that literature and history are in any way shape or form my expertise. I'm just saying that I would definately not approach this subject throught the use of every-day media such as youtube, because that might lead me to create some biased conclusions about a substantially large group of individuals. There is nuance to this stuff... is what I'm trying to say, and is what I wish I would have told Raz. I can't say for sure if Raz believes that absolutely all Islamists have the same ideology and they are all bad, and I was kind of afraid to ask because if he does think that then that would make him 100% racist by definition. And at this point in life, the grand age of 19 to 20 years old, I don't know how much you can change your beliefs, I know Raz is smart so I have hope he can change his beliefs.

And then it happened, some hours later, my mother took Lucas and I to the plaza of Punta Gorda, isn't that wonderful. Sofe and Bruno were not there. we arrrived slightly late at 18:20, but Sofe and Bruno also arrived late so it's all good. I walked with Lucas and I tried discussing this subject with him, but he quickly deflected to saying that the frickin sky was blue or whatever, meaning he probably didn't want to talk about it which is understandable. We walked around until Sofe and Bruno appeared. It was really nice reuniting with some very missed friends.

We start walking through the ramble. I talk to Bruno about my conversation with Raz. Bruno isn't surprised, after all Raz supports the decisions of the current Israeli government, which includes bombs exploding and killing people. Bruno agrees that Muslims do have some bad things as a group, they don't treat women very nice. Many women often complain about how much they need to cover themselves, and women that convert to Islam traditions often regret doing so. Not to mention I read a whole book that extensively covered this global issue. Persepolis by Marijane Satrapi. Raz had mentioned that this religion is relatively new in regard to the others, so maybe they are a little behind in the evolution of women's rights since the other religions got born early and had a head start.

I do severely disagree with the treatment of women, not only in Islam but also in all the other main monotheistic religions. They always seem like accesories or like unimportant to an extent. I wonder when we will move past this, maybe the next pope. Still, I don't really believe that the entirety of the muslim population should be hated because of this, and Bruno agrees. It's dumb to hate any group of people just because of a "might". However in Raz's case, Raz is a jew, and Islam extremists hate jews. Therefore we have a russian roulette situation, where in Raz's case its safer to not trust any Islam at all and assume they are all bad just to be safe and to avoid meetin a potential Islam extremist. Therefore Raz's beliefs can be justified by his innate desire to not die, one desire that I, and hopefully you, also have

With this out of my brain, I can finally, have, some, fun.

What should Sofe do upon finding out the guy that stabbed someone wants his phone number

  1. Try to help this individual work through his problems in hopes of eventually fixing them and living happily ever after

  2. Ignore the problems and hope for the best

The reasonable option would be option C, however Sofe opted for option D. Eventually we get to some random restaurant, we sit down in this random restaurant, and Lucas has an amazing idea. Playing Impostor. Now, I know we have played this a grand total of 2 times already, ones with Fede, another with Raz, and this third time with Sofe and Bruno. I have aquired some skills. So I am going to go into more detail here. The rules art simple

  • A word is chosen
  • An impostor is chosen
  • Everyone but the impostor knows the word
  • Everyone must say one word that relates to the original word, including the impostor
  • The impostor must figure out the word
  • The others must figure out who the impostor is
  • The impostor wins if he guesses the word after being caught
  • The impostor also wins if he doesn't get caught and someone else is wrongfully accused
  • The others will win if they succesfully vote out the impostor without him knowing the secret word

I will only cover the three most interesting games

The Hint Word problem

After a while of playing, we decided to activate hintwords. The word was KFC. Sofe said delicious, I said rabas (fried squid) Lucas said animal, and Bruno said Kentucky. This was a bad sign alreay, but I immediately noticed it was Bruno because he said the actualy word. The right play would have been to act as if that word was suspicious and vote him out then and there to lower his chances of saying KFC. However we played a second round aswell and it became clear that whoever the impostor was, he or she knew that the word was KFC, meaning we had already lost. Still, I think it was pretty smart how I managed to deduce it was Bruno despite him saying Kentucky. It turns out that Bruno got the word "Colonel" making it extremely obvious.

Date: 22/12/2025

Climate: Cloudy

Initial Spacetime: 21:00 Mono

Title: Asade

Before the event

I woke up today thinking about Islams and how true was the dog-hating claims that Raz made yesterday, thus I spent most of the day investigating this. And I came up with a second Document stored in a Portable Format detailing all my research about why the Qu'ran says this. [[SPOILER ALER: It doesn't really]]

Then I get to a very big discussion with Raz about weather or not anyone who believes in Islam is bad and deserves the hate and condemnation of Raziel Meir, a wrath I wouldn't wish upon anyone. It took a while, a huge while. But I managed to get him to agree with something along these lines, "Given that the Muslim individual hasn't interpreted the religious texts in ways that disagree with my[Raz's] personal values, I don't hate him". So that sounds like a really dumb and obvious conclussion we could have gotten to in like 5 minutes.

But most of the 2 hour debate was spent with me trying to convince Raz that it's still possible to interpret the Qu'ran in non-evil ways. Raz believes that in it's core, it can't be, because the religion itself was corrupt, I believed that it wasn't the religion that is corrupt, but mostly the people that are in current control of the main narrative of the religion. He eventually admitted that it may be true that it's not the religion itself that is evil, but instead the most popular interpretation of such religion, aswell as the interpretation of Islam extremists. To disprove my claim, Raz would need to find a verse in the Qu'ran that is undeniably, indisputably, 100% bad, and no context can possibly save it from being bad. I think im in the clear because I don't think that is actually possible. The bible has slavery and buying women, yet the context still saves it from being racist and mysoginist. I very highly doubt that the Qu'ran differs from this in any way, but who am I to know, i'll let Raz look it up.

Anyways, after that, the event begun

I went to Lucas' house, he is doing an Asado tonight and he has invited Dani, Luca, Fabri, and me into his house. I cut the bread, Fabri critiqued our contributions, Luca cut the chorizo, Dani brought the chimichurri, and Lucas cooked the meat. It was wonderful. The meat was really good, Luca brought some cheddar-injected chorizo which was nice. We also played a few rounds of impostor that were really interesting. I'm all alone

Date: 16/01/2026

Climate: Clear

The fact he didn't even respond to that message leads me to think that you are not going to be hearing from him or his Israeli adventures. Except for this one detail, he crossed paths with school counselour Valentina Manzo during his trip.

I also started a small political discussion, which I am getting more comfortable with having, which is a good thing. I know that Raz is somehow always going to believe the opposite of what I believe, which I find entretaining. The subject of discussion is the fact that the US banned Uruguay along with 74 other countries from creating immigrant visa's. The official statement is that they want to diminish "Public Charge" which is a way to refers to the amount of money that the government has to spend on immigrants through public service. If this money isn't net negative then that's bad because the immigrant isn't winning you any money, meaning you loosing money.

However Uruguay is really cool, and all of our migrants are considered low-risk because we tend to be surprisingly productive and well educated. Who would have guessed. It makes sense since we do have the highest standard of living in latin america. Therefore I think that Donald 's decision to ban the creation of immigrant visas from Uruguay was not economically driven. I asked Raz what Uruguay could have done to deserve this.

Raz responded "Communist Government" with no elaboration. I opted for a similarly unelaborated response "No?". Meant to communicate to Raz the fact that our current president is often described as being "center-left" in the political spectrum and so far away from communism you couldn't even see it with a telescope. Raz (who is travelling to Israel at this point) responded after a while with the word "Adjacent".

It was funny the first two times but at this point I start to get tired of this inneficient style of communication, so I deliver to him my full fleshed out opinion for him to either disect, counter, or ignore.

Uruguayan migrants are surprisingly productive according to what i've read, so what are the possible causes towards the decision to do this to Uruguay. One possibility is ideological differences, which is what Raz is suggesting. This is unlikely to me because not only would it be a little petty and immature, but the Uruguayan government is barely skewed to the left. I would understand it more if we were a government of leftist extremists, sure. But that is not the case, we aren't a communist government or anything close/adjacent to it.

Therefore I can only conclude that the US hates Uruguay and thus we must immediately start a war. Whoever strikes first wins... wait... what do you mean we don't have nukes?



Rating meh

Upon some self reflection I realise that by being extremely concise, Raz was either trying to be humorous or trying to signal to me that he doesn't want to talk about this. So he is probably not going to respond, considering how he might actually have better things to do in his fun trip.

Iron Lung

Date: 03/02/2026

Climate: Cold

Space: Pathe Du Mont Movies

Time: 17:30

Today something amazing is going to happen. If you didn't know, incredibly youtuber Markiplier once played Iron Lung, and he liked the story so much that he decided to make a movie about it. The movie was great, I unfortunately don't have much evidence that I was in the movie because I was too occupied actually watching this masterpiece. I liked it a lot, all of it. The only part that threw me off a little bit is a shot of Simon with blood on his face getting mad and destroying the speaker, that close up shot for some reason didn't look that good to me.

Regardless, the movie was spectacular, I liked it a lot. It had some really cool cinematography, all the different angles used to keep the watching entretaining were very effective. All the shots of blood and water pouring through the Iron Lung, any and all scenes outside of the Iron Lung were also really cool. The effects(both practical and not) were all really cool, at no point did I really get thrown off by bad CGI or bad acting of any sort. All the dialogue was very believable and sensical in that situation they were in.I really did feel a lot of suspense, which is what I believe it wanted me to feel. The ending I failed to comprehend a little. But here is my interpretation of it, SPOILER ALERT

The eldritch god tries to convince Simon to join him, telling him that no one else must see the light, only he, and he will be the last one. Simon does not follow the voice, but apparently the voice has powers, and it can control some blood tendrils that capture Simon's arms. He manages to liberate himself off it's grip by... ripping off his arm... yikes. Before doing that, he managed to tie his Black-Box containing Crucial-Information to a Life-Jacker. He destroys the window of the Iron Lung, presumably to let the package flow out. The eldritch voice tries to convince him, it uses the voice of Ava somehow, and it keeps trying to convince him to join the light or whatever, but Simon doesn't and he gets eaten by a fish. However in the end, we see that the balck box floated up and was found.

Now my personal interpretation is the following one. Joining the light could mean several things, for starters it could mean going to wherever everyone who disappeard due to the rapture went, it could also be knowledge, understanding what caused the rapture. It could also just straight up kill you, it could also be all three at the same time. In my opinion it's all three at the same time. Regardless of that, Simon decided to not go gently into that deep night, he instead refused to follow the voices that essentially told him to give up on hope for humanity surviving this, and he succesfully delivered the black box. Another aspect to this whole thing is that the Blood seems toa act to a certain extent like The Mass from white knuckle, it can consume things and incorporate them into itself and use them. This explains how the fish, the blood-vines, and Ava's voice were all working together to stop Simon in his final moments, they were all consumed by the eldritch god of blood or something.

Overall the movie was fantastic, there was a special scene that was a clear reference to the game's original ending where the fish breaks open the Submarine and eats you, I really liked the CGI there, it was very cool. Of course the lore was meant to be confusing and kind of incomplete, it didn't really give you much more than what the game already offered. Simon struggles with constant guilt of having exploded Filament Station. Everything he does is reasonable which is really cool in a suspense/horror movie. It definately has a lot of metaphorical shit and room for interpretation and whatnot, but overall it was a cool movie that dealt with the themes of hopelessness, guilt, and selflessness.

Some Media of the Iron Lung Movie




Rating of the movie 8.1/10

Good for Mark's first movie, hope he does more.

He argumented that if Ross hadn't shot her, maybe she wouldn't have changed her trajectory as much, causing Ross to get more injured.

Now it's known that a living person has more control over a vehicle than a dead person. That's why it's common police training to not shoot at moving vehicles, it's always better to let them escape. This is because shooting at them will very likely cause the car to start accelerating out of control and crash onto something/someone, basically turning the car into a massive mass of high speed dangrousness. So essentially shooting a moving vehicle to stop it from harming people is dumb and goes against Logic and common police training meant to keep the streets safe.

Using this argument, I tried to relay to Raz just how dumb it is to shoot a moving vehicle in hopes of stopping it from causing harm. Raz kind of started to concede and recognize that the officer might not have taken the best course of action in this situation. After hammering on a little bit more the full extent of the dumbness that shooting a moving vehicle entails, Raz conceded that the officer should probably lose his licence. He still believed that Good was the one who was mostly at fault for this tragedy, that's something I can get behind, I don't exactly agree with it but I can understand how one could reach such conclusion.

So, I we both reached a consensus. "Ms Good lacked the SITUATIONAL AWARENESS necesary to keep the streets safe while using a vehicle, thus (if she was still alive) she should have lost her license. The officer lacked the QUICK CRITICAL THINKING SKILLS required on the field keep the streets safe. Thus he should lose his license". Emmy Noether

I know her mostly because of her workd in the conservation laws regarding relativity. Einstein simply couldn't exactly figure out how energy was conserved in a sistem with bent space time. She miraculously figured out an amazing fact through hard work and math. She discovered that translational symmetry is what causes conservation of momentum, rotational symmetry causes conservation of angular momentum, and time symmetry gives you conservation of energy!!! This were big revelations at the time, specially the last one. This is because on the long term, there is no time symmetry, and that explains one of the most unexplainable phenomena of all, the redshifting of light in space!!! Why does it lose energy??? where does the energy go???? Einstein could not figure it out, but Noether could, she simply figured that the energy is lost because of the lack of time symmetry. And if not lost, then it goes to the fabric of spacetime to keep it expanding or whatever. Truly genius stuff. She also made discoveries about local symmetries, and also discovering where energy goes in bent space time and such, proving that the Bianchi Identities were simply the best solution there was to get. She was second woman in Germany to get a doctorate, she managed to get a small salary for teaching at a university. Until the Nazis came and banned jews from teaching. But even still, she gave lectures in her Home Kitchen, and he would even teach Nazi Students because she would not discriminate at all. He would spread her knowledge and passion for science to anyone willing to uncover the truth, even if ideologically disaligned. When it comes to being a genius, she is simply the best there is!!!!

I believe women play life on Hard Mode, they have so much more going against them than men. They have more challenges to overcome, and I think that's awesome. Actually no, it's really bad, the awesome part is that they are actually succesfull at overcoming the challenges sometimes. But I guess I still have many challenges to overcome, I have Crohns disease, ADHD, Depression, and Anxiety. I guess we all have our challenges.

Time: Middle of the day

On a more serious note I have been hearing some interesting stuff about Iran. Israel and the US claim that for what I think is the eleventh time, Iran is building a weapon of mass destruction (Nuke) and they have to stop them. The IAEA noticed that Iran was enriching a bunch of Uraniu, this was (according to Iran) a retalliatory action to the sanctions that the US had put on Iran, but it was only to show everyone that they have the ability to make Nukes, not necesairly the intention to. They said that if the US lifts the sanction, they will reverse this process and stop enriching so much Uranium.

But the US and Israel didn't take this threat of Iran having the capability of nuclear bombs lightly, so Israel sabotaged (bombed) the Natanz Uranium enrichment facility on April 2021. Iran also didn't take this threat lightly, so they enriched even more Uranium, up to 441kg of 60% Uranium. Not exactly weapon grade percentage but still a lot of fuel and it can be enriched further to make weapons. And that brings us to today where Israel and the US have just about had it with these Uranium enriching shennanigans.

I was going to call this the "Retard'o Vial" but that didn't make much sense. However, I will use this opportunity to do something

To take a stance. A stance on slurs, more specifically the word "Retarded". Intellectually disabled people in the past were referred to with the term "Mental Retardation". But that term wasn't very helpful since it was only purely descriptive of someone who by the societal standards of the time, was seen as less efficient or wrong in a way. Therefore the word "Retarded" was not only used in medical contexts to basically say "Your child has no hope in this world" but it was also used as an insult to people who acted in a way that they viewed as "wrong".

But now the term "Mental Retardation" got fuckin discombobulated out of the medical realm, by which I mean, it doesn't exist anymore. Therefore, there is no longer anyone in the world who is officially retarded (unless they kept a diagnosis for mental retardation from 15 years ago). They can have Autism, ADHD, Dyslexia, you name it, but they aren't retarded. However the word has persisted through it's vanishment from the medical realm, in the form of an insult. For a small while it was used to still refer to intellectually disabled people, but as it became clear that these people can still be capable of great things, people started to use it basically as a synonym for dumb.

This is where we are at right now, the word "Retarded" is a synonym for "Dumb" or "a delayed way of thinking" as I like to put it. When I say "damn, this war sure is retarded" I am obviously not saying that the war is intellectualy disabled, neither am I implicitly suggesting that wars are caused by intellectualy disabled people, or that they are comparable to intellectual disability at all. I am saying they are senseless or stupid. This is actually very similar to the words "Moron", "Imbecile", and "Inept" which all used to be medical terms to describe low IQ people, just like "Mental Retardation". However with time, all of these words just became normal insults and ways of just referring to inneficient or wrong processes. I believe that the word "Retarded" is on it's way to becoming just another normal insultive word, a synonym for dumb, moronic, or imbecilic. It's just that some people are still touchy about the word, because only recently 15 years ago did the term "Mental Retardation" get changed to "Intellectual Disability" but I am sure that in some years, the word will get neutered out of all of it's slurish, discriminant meaning, and it will just be another insult.

So I decided to step ahead of the curve and start using the word "Retarded" as a normal insult, because I just happen to really like how the word sounds, and how it's actually a synonym for delayed. That's actually another point, retarded means delayed, before all this medical nonsense got coined. You can still see it in several academic topics such as the topic of Retarded Potentials in physics, which describes electromagnetid fields, or a retard in music which means to slow down the tempo, or a flame retardant. What I am getting at is that we can't really treat this word as that much of an insult because actually retarded people don't really exist anymore, and furthermore, the word has an actual meaning that is used, or used to be used, in several ways. It's not like the N-word which was created explicitly to refer what the people at the time believed to be a lower race of human beings.

My next point is about slurs in general. The word "Guy" originated from Guy Fawkes, he was a man that tried to blow up the British Parliament, and thus he was seen as a bad figure(I promise I am getting somewhere with this). So then the word "Guy" became basically an insult that was meant to comparing some individual to Guy fawkes. But as time went on, it was used so often that it lost it's insultivity attribute, and thus guy became just a word for any male human, and eventually, any human.

My point with this, is that by letting an insultive word be used as an insult, it will eventually lose it's insultivity value, and thus it won't be capable of hurting anyone anymore. This is was is pseudo-happening with the N-Word, and how black people use to refer to themselves. However by not allowing anyone else to use it either, the word still carries some insultivity to it, and thus it can still be used to insult others. My main point with this is that by restricting people from using a certain insultive word, we are preventing the insultivity value of such a word from decreasing, and thus it will remain a slur, and a weapon, for racist people to use, forever. Therefore, we just shouldn't limit anyone's freedom of speech, if they want to be insultive, they can, they'll be hated for it anyway. Eventually black people won't even be bothered by people calling them the N-word, hell, it might even become a synonym for "guy" if we stopped caring about it so much.

My last point is that I am actually technically intellectually disabled. Which is to say I have ADHD and Autism. Therefore if nothing I said previously made any sense, I can reclaim the word "Retard" just like black people reclaim the N-word, and I am allowed to use it how I please :p

And with all that said, the vial's name is officially the Retard'o Vial, and the liquid within it, is the retard'o fluid. And it has absolutely NOTHING, NOTHING, NOT A THING, NOT A SMIDGET, OR AN IOTA, to do with intellectualy disabled people. It's just dumb

Epic Update

Date: 22/04/2026

FixDate: 28/04/2026

Climate: Cloudy

Space: Living Room

Time: 12:39

Today I have a grand total of 9 tasks to accomplish. Furthermore, I have been thinking a lot lately, a lot about politics. I've been getting more and more informed about every subject every. I've been gaining so much knowledge, I kept trying to make this a big deal to my friends but I really don't think they care :/ But that doesn't matter, because I care. Thing is, i've come to some political conclusions, I have decided that this day, I will fully disclose them in this very entry. Furthermore, I will not be using any of the following language.

  • Left
  • Right
  • Republican
  • Democrat
  • Socialist
  • Communist
  • Capitalist

Because my affiliation with any of those has absolutely no relation to the party itself, it has everything to do with what the party has to offer. No biases involved. That being said, here I go.

I have one philosophy that has followed me all my life. Helping is good. My theories indicate that this philosophy stemmed from my family's religious following, Christianity. Jesus Christ as described in the bible seems to have been an indredible individual. He always helped, and he always managed to defeat opressors through the means of sacrifice as opposed to violence. Now I am incredibly confident that Christianity as a whole has been twisted and turned so much to the point that anyone can believe in it and make it make sense, regardless of weather or not their believes are compatible with the original beliefs of Jesus.

But according to my interpretation of the bible (which is obviously "the best") Jesus seems to have been the following

  • Promoted love and peace to everyone
  • Was against richness as a concept
  • Condemned violence
  • Helping people

He was really fecking epic. My interpretation of Jesus basically focuses on Jesus himself, using all of the stories of his apostoles to construct Jesus and his beliefs. So helping people is a really big thing in Christianity. And I believe that it's the most important thing in all of Christianity.

Therefore and ideal government would be one that helps people. I am really glad we could all come to this conclusion. And you should be really glad that I went on that very necesary tangent about Jesus Christ to inform you about why helping people is good.

Obviously in order to help people, the government is going to need some sort of hierarchy/system. And this is the big divide between most politicians, I will call these philosophies 1 and 2. Some people say that the government should just let the people do their own thing and everything will turn great, someone sometime ago wrote something about an invisible hand, this is what he(or she[or they]) was[were] talking about(I am almost 100% sure it was a he and I just did that to ragebait someone, I don't even know who). Then there are the people who believe that the government should be responsible for providing the basic needs that people need, this would include things such as the ultra survivalist 101 basics(food, shelter and water) although some people often tag on things such as safety and healthcare. Obviously to do this, the government needs to obtain resources from somewhere, they would do this by establishing some intense taxes.

These are the two of the most famous Governmental philosphies that go under two aforementioned names that I refuse to utter. And two respective parties whom were attributed some directional nomenclature are tied to these philosophies. So which one of these philosophies is better. I'll tell you which one, I think that the one where the government collects and provides is better. Nowadays, all governments tend to be a combination of both of these philosophies, since as far as I know, all governments have taxes.

If I had to chose only one of those, I would definately go for the system where the government collects money and provides the people cool stuff(Philosophy 2). Mainly because putting all of the control in the people is kinda dangerous, there are a lot of people, and some of them are kinda evil. The government tends to be smaller than the population, and the government workers tend to be selected by rather rigorous procedures. That is not to say that government corruption can't happen, that would be a dumb thing to say, mainly because of how many times it has been proven untrue.

So nice, you got my opinion there :D I prefer more taxes if it means the government will do cool stuff like free education and free healthcare (and free survival essentials for those in need). But let's actually look at some real-world examples and see the stuff.

THE US

So, the US, in my opinion, has kinda shot itself in the foot as of recently. They took the worst part about the two philosophies and combined them to make the worst thing imaginable. Okay I am exagerating a lot, but I'll explain what I mean. The worst part about Philosophy 1 is that it very easily allows anyone to create to do whatever they want. Some people who happen to have both the SMART and EVIL attributes will be capable of doing some evil stuff to gain insurmountable amounts of power. The worst part about the second philosophy is essentially the same thing, but instead it's the government that gains insurmountable amounts of power, and they basically end up in a dictatorship which like.... it's bad, freedom is always a valuable thing.

The US has now gotten both of these bad things. They have incredibly wealthy individuals like Elon Musk and Bill Gates and Jeff Bezos and formerly Jeffrey Epstein. And the worst part of it all is this wealth individuals have so much power, that they can actually interfere with the government. The best example is Donald 's whole DOGE thing with Elon Musk. Actually never-fucking-mind, the best example is obviously Jeffrey Epstein, wtf was I talking about?? Jeffrey Epstein had so much influence in the government, that his influence persists even after his death. People that are basically confirmed criminals such as Kash Patel who definately committed perjury regarding the whole case. And that leads me to the fact that certain government actions in recent US politics, the government corruption. Donald has passed a little something called Schedule F, something that Biden had gotten rid off because it was dumb, and Donald decided to unsurprisingly re-establish. It basically makes it easier to fire people from government entities like the DOJ. This means that members of such entities will obviously be pressured to not go against what the current government is doing, unless they want to get fired. That is not smart. This leads to stuff like the Renee Good accident, not the accident itself mind you, yes it's a tragedy, we can all agree on this, but the more concerning part is the DOJ declared it self-defense with no court or trial or anything. And the FBI confiscated all the evidence so no one could sue them. And Christi Noem declared that the victim was a terrorist. All of these actions point to one fact, no one is going against the government because it was given too much power. I honestly think this all could be much, much worst. Donald right now is focusing on basically kicking out unregistered immigrants, which isn't their most pertinent problem by a landslide, but it's a problem nonetheless and he is focusing on it. The degrees of success may vary, but he is trying his best.

Okay wow, so anyways. The Donald Administration + The Freedom granted to individuals has caused both supermassive rich and powerfull evil, and super a powerful government that no one can properly oppose. Having so much wealth and power in the hands of such few individuals, is bad. I am not even claiming that these individuals are necesairly evil, but their biases will still have monumental impacts on everyone, every single decision they make. Decisions this big should be approved by like congress or something. Like Donald going to kidnapping Maduro or going to War with Iran, those kinds of decisions are just too big for a small collection of people to take.

Nordic Countries

Take for example, Finland, they are really cool. They have high taxes, but their government is super great and innovative. They have cool healthcare, and cool education, and stuff like that. There is a lot of trust in the government and thus, people aren't afraid to pay taxes. Same goes for the Neatherlands. They have a ton of things you can apply for to reduce the cost of living. For example Fede, since he is working and studying at the same time, it turns out that he was able to apply for some government thing which basically made his tuition free. That is really good because during that time his father was refusing to pay his tuition for some family issues. Also their public transport is ultra-cool. But enouph glazing, this is the Philosophy 2 stuff that is cool. However there are obviously bad examples to Philosophy 2 of course. Just take a look as Kischners Argentina, they were fuckin terrible, and I fear that anyone that attempts to defend them is immediately wrong, I'm sorry if you are reading this Fede, I know about your partisan affiliations but sometimes people are just evil, and Kischner was just evil. She manipulated the working class into voting for her and then she stole an approximate shit ton of money and left. I also believe that Uruguay doesn't have the best Philosophy 2 Structure. It's government is wayyyyyyyyy to big for such a small country, so big that, it actually kinda becomes useless? It feels as if the government is creating more branches for the sole purpose of creating more government jobs. This just makes things more and more expensive which overall kinda sucks. It also creates a massive middle-class shortage since only those who basically live-off the government and the riches people can live.

And also I am not going to pretend there are no succesfull philosophy 1 countries. The US was succesfull for quite a while up until now. And I am sure there are other examples that I simply don't know about :p but hey. This is my major and most important conclusion. Listen up and down because this one is a banger and everyone should listen.

IT DOESN'T MATTER!!!

And I physically, mentally, and emotionally can not stress enouph how much it doesn't fucking matter. I don't know if you noticed, but those among you who have actually been paying attention must have realised that both philosophies have the same exact problems, which is the unequal distribution of power to a small selection of people. This can happen regardless of what system you use, regardless of capitalism or socialism. Yes I know I wasn't supposed to say those but I need this to be clear as crystals. Global Sumud Flotilla Interception !!

This flotilla was created in 2025 to aid the innocent citizens of Gaza who were getting retaliatorily bombed because of the actions of Hamas.

Flotilla's claims

The flotilla claims themselves to be a humanitarian organisation funded in spain with the sole goal of helping Gaza through non-violent strategies such as giving them sources of food. They have a website that keeps track of all their aid-ships and how many of them have been intercepted by Israel. They also upload livestreams and pictures into the website

Israel claims

Israel claims that the flotilla is actually a massive PR stunt funded by Hamas through indirect insiduous means. The flotilla is meant to exagerate the extent to which Gaza citizens have suffered, thus giving them more international support and resources that they can use to gain an upper hand. In reality, the ships don't even have humanitarian aid, and they are just there to spread propaganda and mock Israel. And if they do have humanitarian aid, it's just a "symbolic" amount rather than a "functional" amount. This means that they can stop them legally without it being a war-crime.

  • Renne Good was there to aggrivate the guards
  • Renne Good was trying to run him over
  • Officer Ross thought he could prevent damage with a gun

And that last one is kind of a trick, because if he did think that, then he would have been wrong, aswell as in violation of basic police training (don't shoot the passanger in moving vehicles). Policemen are meant to keep people safe and use weapons responsibly, this was not a responsible use of weapons, there was nothing to be gained from firing a weapon in this specific situation, and that's why the one who fired the weapon, is at fault, for her death. If I ever discuss this with Raz again, I will just tell him that, because it's the very bottom of my analysis. There was no reason to pull out a gun, let alone fire it... if he hadn't pulled and fired his gun, no one would have died.

Was there anything wrong with her presence there?? These are questions we simply do not have the answer to because of the aforementioned lack of investigation. Thus we can assume that in the worst case scenario, she was blocking the path of ICE and constantly interfering with their operations. In this scenario, I still do not believe it is mostly the fault of Renne Good, she shouldn't have died even if she was interfering with ICE. She should have been arrested, she should have had police officers called to the scene, she shouldn't have been shot by an ICE agent. That circumstance was entirely born out of Ross' action to pull a gun out and fire it.

I have the feeling this is my final conclussion on the case, unless I re-visit this case next time. But I am so confident on this. Like even if she was interfering, she was most definately not threatening to kill anyone. Or at least from the looks of it. Also the lack of an investigation really speaks volumes that I am not willing to address here because we are only talking about the situation itself.

I can only think that Raz came to the conclusion that Renne was mostly at fault due to bias. No matter how I pose it, no matter what kind of conservative values I use. Like even if Renne Good genuinely was the worst, no video evidence shows her doing anything harmful. I am convinced that it was a massive slip from Ross to shoot her. Like a massive one. Even if she was there purposefully interfering, like, Ross had recorded their license. If she refused to get out and escaped the police on purpose, then they would have found her anyways, and put her to a trial. He had the lethal weapon and thus the responsability, shooting Renne good protected no one, as I always said, nothing was gained from shooting her.

So IF the officer thought Renne Good was using the car as a weapon, shooting it is still not a good idea. I literally see no way in which it's mostly Good's fault. The Play

Some epic scenes

The play was really good in my opinion. It was about this guy called Lorenzo whose father abandoned him and his best friend Isabelle died :( They moved to montevideo so he could escape the memories of his fallen friend. He has a sister called Martina and together they fight against the evils facilitated by the SOCIETALLY DIGITAL connection that modern technological devices provide us with. They connect us to everyone, and disconnect us from everyone.

Martina is in love with epic social media celebrity Tiago. But Tiago sent her a SUSPICIOUS PICTURE, and he demmanded for a SUSPICIOUS PICTURE of her own. Martina refused at first, but gave in to his demmands after pressure from Tiago and fear of losing him(she must have been really in love{also Martina's and Lorenzo's father left when they were young so maybe Martina fears abandonment}) So Martina gave into the pressure and sends him a SUSPICIOUS PICTURE of her own. It's not long before Tiago increases his EVILNESS ATTRIBUTE by evolving from requesting SUSPICIOUS PICTURES to requesting SUSPICIOUS ACTIVITIES(sex) from Martina, but Martina refuses, and Tiago retalliates by posting her nudes :0

Meanwhile, Lorenzo is also a main character in all of this. He's got this hero complex because he couldn't save her best friend Isabelle. He tries to open up this sort of shrink for his classmates where they can all talk about their problems. But it's just not working brooooooo, nobody wants to hear about this douche and his problems. He spends most of his time alone except for this one girl with a yellow dress who gives him some advice, but she is always on the phone which he find severely annoying. Eventually Lorenzo decides to ask Tiago to use his HIGH SOCIAL MEDIA STATUS to promote Lorenzo's shrink. Tiago does so in exchange for putting in a good word for him, to his sister, Martina...

So the psycology sessions go well until this guy called Nacho gets trolled by these trolls into thinking that the girl he loves has confessed to her via chat-message. They utilize Artificial Intelligence to create credible evidence that it's actually her crush(The Crush's name is Pili). This leads to an incredibly embarassing serenade in the middle of the class from Nacho to Pili

"Sos caca de pajaro? Por que caiste del cielo, y no puedo sacarte de mi cabeza"

"Sos el dedo corto de mi pie? Por que te quiero dar contra todos los rincones"

-Nacho from "Disconnected"

If you know spanish, you will probably realize this confession went sub-optimally, except. Not really. Because after that embarassment, Pili and Nacho had a serious 1-1 where they discussed what had just happened. Nacho admitted he got his ass trolled by some trolls, but he genuinely fell in love with Pili 6 years ago because of her confident self, and not because she is popular online.Pili liked this, and now they are in love, but in secret, because Pili can't be seen hanging out with someone of low social status. Nacho's social status got destroyed after that embarassing confession.

Nacho also got mad at Lorenzo because he was the one who told Nacho to confess to her. Because Nacho remembers the fact that Isa and him had a fight right before Isa died, and he regrets never solving the conflict before he couldn't go back :( So Lolo told Nacho to confess to Pili, but that went poorly at first, and Nacho blamed Lolo. But Lolo doesn't know that he actually helped him in the end. Which is really epic but it also means Lolo is severely depressed because he thinks Nacho is mad and also Pili won't go to his shrink no more because she finally found a man who lover he for who she really is (Nacho). So Lorenzo confides about all of this with Yellow Dress Girl while they drink Mate together, but Lolo gets annoyed even at her because she is always with her phone!!

Pili and Martina have also been friends all along, and they often talk to each other a lot aswell. I just forgot to mention that all up until now. So now that Martina's nudes have been published online, and people are under the impression that she posted them, everyone thinks she is "gifted", which doesn't mean that she has some special talent, in spanish, the adjective "gifted" is used to describe someone that "gifts" her body to others very easily, which is to say a slut. And everyone treats her very poorly for this, it's getting to her real hard, and worst of all, Tiago actually helped Lorenzo, so Lorenzo believes she published that picture by herself too :0 which is the narrative that Tiago is promoting. And it's also really bad for Martina's mental health to be betrayed this hard by her own brother. She's only got Pili now, and Pili tries helping her but Martina pushes her away in frustration, and Pili gets frustrated too so she leaves her.

Eventually, the pressure of ruining everything gets to Lorenzo, from his perspective, he failed Nacho, and he just called her sister a slut or how we say it in spanish, a "puta". He even tries to talk to the yellow dress girl that is always there for him, but she won't get off the darn phone!!! Lorenzo encounters Tiago and asks him if he was the one who released Martina's nudes, Tiago has a hard time admitting this fact, but Lorenzo figures out the truth by analysing his guilty expression, so Lorenzo saves him the effort by delivering an answer via a fast moving fist towards Tiago's face. Lorenzo now realises that the only person he has left is his sister. So he runs to her right as she is having an epic MENTAL BREAKDOWN induced by the depravity of her situation. They use each other's bonds to perservere through each other's mental breakdowns. The mother sees this and is obviously worried by the whole scene, so the kids explain everything.

The mother does what any sensible person would have immediately done after witnessing some classic CYBER-BULLYING, he takes the matter, to the principal's office. The very next day, Tiago is expelled and he gets into a fight with Lorenzo, but Lorenzo is backed up by Pili, Martina, and Nacho. Tiago gives the fuck up, and throws his phone with HIGH SOCIAL MEDIA FOLLOWING onto the ground.

Lorenzo uses his phone to deliver a widespread message about his story, in full detail. He was best friends with a girl named Isa, they were always together, never seen apart, they did EVERYTHING together. They always walked back home together since they lived close to each other, and Isa was his only friend because everyone else was apparently an ass that made fun of Martina and Lorenzo because their father left them. But one day Lorenzo and Isa got in a fight and they both decided to take seperate paths to their homes. While taking the seperate paths, they were still fighting with each other through SOCIAL MEDIA. This proved fatal because Isa was too distracted with her online fewd with Lolo to realise there was a truck about to end her life. Lorenzo was devastated at the entire situation, his family moved out, and he stopped using phones for the rest of his life.

That is the saddest story ever. After Lolo's revelation, Yellow Dress Girl enters the scene, she informs Lorenzo that she must go, for he doesn't need her no more. The audience is shocked at the pretty-obvious-yet-still-super-sad revelation that the yellow dress girl was Lorenzo's brain ghost hallucination of Isa all along!!! It's something I theorised when I realised that no one but Lorenzo would ever talk to the yellow dress girl. But I didn't actually expect it to be true!!! That just makes this shit even sadder D:

So brain ghost Isa says that Lorenzo doesn't need her anymore, and thus she must depart. He is devastated by this, but Nacho, Pili, and Martina are there to console him.

"I know you like to imagine that she is still here by your side, but you've got us now"

Ohhhh, that quote made me shed a tear. It was all done so beautifully. I mean like, they hinted at it very well. And they even made Lorenzo use similar expressions, like comparing how he could make the teacher go on tangents that go on and on and on like A TRUCK!!!!! And also saying how he seems to be having a bad break that goes on and on and on like a WHEEL. And both times, he is talking to Yellow Dress Girl, AKA brain ghost Isa. I don't even know if that was done on purpose but it was so gooooooooooood, and so sadddddd.

The stroy ends with the main four connected

  • Martina is now on good terms with Lorenzo and her bffsy Pili
  • Pili is in good terms with Martina and Lorenzo(Lorenzo helped her with psycology stuff) and also she is in love with Nacho
  • Nacho is in love with Pili and good friends with Lorenzo
  • Lorenzo is in good terms with everyone, and he finally let go off brain ghost Isa

honestly that was spectacular, super good, excellent stuff right here, this is the shit I love to see in theatre, this is some true DIGITAL SOCIETY CRITIQUE MASTERPIECE. 10/10, honestly, just. muah *Chef's kiss*

In order to calculate the litrocity of these events, I would need to define how much litrocity there is per dollar wasted, and I'm not doing that. SO therefore there is no litrocity, because this is too pertinent to economics which is not in my field of interest. They call it the anti-weaponization fund, funded by taxpayers.
